msg:It is the most expensive B&B in Pingtan Island (including all big hotels). To be honest, the location of the hotel is very good and the scenery is good, but I believe that most travelers choose this hotel because it takes photos. To be honest, this is its only two advantages (the other is breakfast, which is also good!) Itâ€™s really great for taking photos! But other than that, nothing is worth the price!
Hygiene: The toiletries look quite high-end, but if you look closely, the sealing stickers on all the small bottle mouths are broken (indicating that these disposable items are actually added repeatedly), the cleanliness of the bathroom is average, and rust stains can be seen everywhere on the sink. There are no disposable slippers either!
Environment: The sound insulation effect of the room is very poor, the door gap is about 2 centimeters, and there are many people traveling and shooting, so it is very noisy.
Service: The hotel provides travel photography for non-hotel guests, so it will be very noisy. If you just want to take photos and check in at the hotel, you can save some money and stay in a hotel with better facilities, and then go to the hotel to take travel photos.
Facilities: The hot water will take about half an hour to heat up
If you just want to see the scenery, it is recommended that you stay in the hotel in front of the hotel. The location of that hotel is even better, directly facing the sea without any obstruction.
By the way, I checked today and found that the package we ordered came with afternoon tea, but it has been 5 days since we checked out, and no one has mentioned where the afternoon tea is.
All in all, I should stay here once in my life and sleep by the sea.
However, you will only sleep by the sea once in your life!
